- Changed `projects/hanwoo-dashboard/src/auth.js`: unauthenticated protected routes now return an explicit login `NextResponse.redirect()` and reconstruct callback origin from `x-forwarded-proto`, `x-forwarded-host`, and `host` headers before setting `callbackUrl`.

## 2026-06-08 - Codex

- Completed T-1640 as an auto-research selector dirty-plan freshness fix.
- Reproduced the bug with live artifacts: after regenerating `.tmp/scoped-dirty-worktree-handoff-plan-current.json` to dirty count `83` and signature `cd4247dbc9342513840b311645a67368c8962134a47188af1ffe2f7b5d6c8b7b`, `next_experiment_selector.py --dirty-handoff-plan ...` still returned `status=candidate`, selected `dirty_worktree_handoff`, and reported `adoptable_candidate_count=1`.
- Root cause: `_dirty_handoff_plan_matches_inventory()` treated `freshness.current` as current-plan validity, but `dirty_worktree_handoff_plan.py` uses `freshness` to describe whether the previous plan matched the newly generated plan. A newly generated current plan can show previous-plan `stale` while its own dirty signature exactly matches the current GitHub inventory.
- Fixed `next_experiment_selector.py` to treat exact dirty-count and dirty-path signature matching as the current-plan validity signal, require both plan and inventory paths to be available, and keep `freshness` as evidence only.
- Added `workspace/tests/test_auto_research_next_experiment_selector.py` coverage for a matching dirty handoff signature with `freshness=stale` blocking repeated handoff generation.
- Verification passed focused selector pytest (`20 passed`), related selector/debug-inventory/launch pytest (`71 passed`), Ruff format/check for touched files, `py_compile`, path-limited `git diff --check` with CRLF warnings only, and live selector now returns `status=blocked`, `selected_kind=dirty_worktree_handoff_current`, `adoptable_candidate_count=0`.
- Graph detect risk is `0.00`; full dirty-tree `code_review_gate.py --base HEAD --json` remains advisory WARN (`risk_score=0.55`) due broad pre-existing WIP/untracked graph-relevant files. Removed `.tmp/pytest-t1639-*`; no staging, commit, push, revert, `update_goal`, or Hanwoo T-251 retry was performed.

## 2026-06-08 - Codex

- Completed T-1713 as a `claude-goal` invoke help non-mutating UX fix in `claude-goal/` on branch `improve/goal-system`.
- Direct CLI use reproduced that `python goal/scripts/claude_goal.py invoke --help` behaved like a new objective instead of help, printing `Action: set` and storing `Objective: --help` in the active goal DB.
- Cleared the accidental default DB row created during reproduction, then used isolated temp goal DBs for all follow-up reproduction and verification.
- Root cause: `invoke` uses `argparse.REMAINDER`, and the legacy `invoke` dispatch path passed `--help` through to slash-command parsing before argparse help handling, so unknown command text fell through to `set_goal()`.
- Fixed `goal/scripts/claude_goal.py` with non-mutating `INVOKE_HELP` handling for `invoke -h/--help` in both main and legacy invoke paths.
- Added `tests/test_claude_goal.py::test_invoke_help_is_non_mutating` to lock that `--help` and `-h` show help, do not print `Action: set`, and leave `status` at no active goal.
- Verification passed direct temp-DB CLI QA in `.tmp/claude-goal-t1713-cli-qa.json`, focused pytest (`1 passed, 94 deselected`), full claude-goal pytest (`136 passed`), Ruff check, Ruff format check (`9 files already formatted`), py_compile, `git diff --check` with existing CRLF warnings only, and graph detect risk `0.00`.

## 2026-06-08 - Codex

- Completed T-1716 as a `claude-goal` direct `set` help non-mutating UX fix in `claude-goal/` on branch `improve/goal-system`.
- Reproduced the bug with a direct CLI help mutation scan and isolated temp goal DBs: `python goal/scripts/claude_goal.py set --help` returned `0` but printed `Action: set` and stored an active goal whose objective was `--help`; `set -h` had the same state-mutation risk.
- Root cause: `_run_legacy_main_command()` intercepts legacy `set` before argparse, and because `set` uses raw/remainder-style objective text, `--help` was treated as objective content instead of being passed to the direct `set` argparse help renderer.
- Fixed `goal/scripts/claude_goal.py` by letting legacy `set -h/--help` fall through to the existing argparse parser.
- Added `tests/test_claude_goal.py::test_set_help_is_non_mutating` to lock that direct `set --help` and `set -h` show help, do not print `Action: set`, and leave no active goal.
- Verification passed the original repro after the fix (`usage: claude_goal.py set`, no active goal), focused help pytest (`3 passed, 95 deselected` after formatting rerun), full claude-goal pytest (`139 passed`), Ruff check, Ruff format check (`9 files already formatted`), py_compile, `git diff --check` with existing CRLF warnings only, and graph detect risk `0.00`.
- Removed this loop's temp repro and pytest basetemp directories after path-safety verification. No staging, commit, push, revert, `update_goal`, root product edit, or Hanwoo T-251 retry was performed.

- Continued the `/goal` reproduce -> isolate -> root-cause -> fix -> verify loop while preserving existing nested WIP and the completed T-1744 installer malformed Stop entry surface; did not stage nested code, push, revert, call `update_goal`, edit root product code, or retry Hanwoo T-251.

- Continued the `/goal` reproduce -> isolate -> root-cause -> fix -> verify loop while preserving existing nested WIP and the completed T-1747b/T-1748 surfaces; did not stage nested code, push, revert, call `update_goal`, edit root product code, or retry Hanwoo T-251.
- 0-step refresh prioritized a structured-output data-integrity bug over lower-impact message-order differences.
- Reproduced with isolated DB state that `goals.metadata_json = '{broken'` made `json`/`contract` return exit `2` with raw JSON parser text and no `metadata_json` context, while `metadata_json = '[]'` or `"string"` made `json` and `contract` return exit `0` with schema-invalid `metadata` array/string values; `contract --verify-json` accepted those artifacts when the same corrupt DB value was present.
- Root cause: `row_to_dict()` trusted `metadata_json` and passed any decoded JSON value through, while operating-contract verification only checked that `current_goal` was an object and did not enforce `current_goal.metadata` object shape.
- Fixed `goal/scripts/claude_goal.py` by adding `goal_metadata()` validation and rejecting non-object `current_goal.metadata`.
- Added `tests/test_claude_goal.py::test_goal_metadata_json_must_be_object_for_structured_outputs` and `tests/test_claude_goal.py::test_goal_contract_verify_json_rejects_current_goal_metadata_type`.
- Direct after-fix QA in `.tmp/claude-goal-t1749-metadata-json-shape-qa.json` confirms malformed `metadata_json` now returns contextual metadata errors, `json`/direct `contract`/slash `invoke contract`/`doctor --json` leave stdout empty and print no traceback, and operating-contract verification rejects `current_goal.metadata` array values.
- Verification passed focused metadata/contract pytest (`4 passed`), post-format focused rerun (`2 passed`), full isolated pytest with `PYTHONUTF8=1` (`189 passed`), Ruff check, scoped Ruff format check (`9 files already formatted`), py_compile, `git diff --check` with existing CRLF warnings only, and graph detect risk `0.00`.

## 2026-06-09 - Codex

- Completed T-1752 as a `claude-goal` direct artifact-option empty-value parity fix in `claude-goal/` on branch `improve/goal-system`, preserving existing nested WIP and the concurrently recorded T-1751 goal-record schema guard.
- Direct CLI interaction reproduced that `contract --verify-json=`, `contract --json-output=`, `contract --markdown-output=`, `contract --verify-schema=`, `doctor --install --verify-json=`, `doctor --install --json-output=`, `doctor --install --markdown-output=`, and `doctor --install --verify-markdown=` treated empty inline values as omitted and returned normal output or later dependency behavior instead of a value-required usage error.
- Equivalent slash `invoke` paths already rejected those empty values, so the defect was classified as 기능 오류 + 로딩/피드백 + 카피 caused by direct/slash parser policy drift.
- Official references checked: Python argparse value options and invalid-argument behavior, Click option value behavior, and GitHub CLI reference style; the adopted design was to make direct value options fail explicitly instead of silently ignoring user-supplied empty values.
- Fixed `goal/scripts/claude_goal.py` by validating direct `doctor` and `contract` namespace value options with `_validate_option_value()`, matching slash parser behavior.
- Added `tests/test_claude_goal.py::test_direct_artifact_options_reject_empty_inline_values_without_mutating`.

- No nested code staging, push, revert, `update_goal`, root product edit, or Hanwoo T-251 retry was performed.

## 2026-06-09 - Codex

- Completed T-1754 as a `claude-goal` stale-days empty-value guard fix in `claude-goal/` on branch `improve/goal-system`, preserving existing nested WIP and the concurrently recorded T-1753 direct JSON empty session-id parity surface.
- Direct CLI reproduction showed `doctor --stale-days= --json`, `pause-stale --stale-days= --json`, and split-empty `--stale-days ""` variants reached inconsistent feedback: direct commands exposed argparse `invalid int value: ''`, while slash `invoke` paths classified the same empty value as `--stale-days must be an integer`.
- Confirmed the correct behavior should be a missing-value usage error before DB open, with empty stdout, no traceback, and no state mutation.
- Root cause: `_parse_stale_days_value()` called `int(value)` without first validating blank values, and direct `doctor`/`pause-stale` argparse definitions used `type=int`, so empty strings were consumed before the shared option validator.
- Fixed `goal/scripts/claude_goal.py` by routing direct stale-days values through `_parse_stale_days_value()`, validating blank values with `_validate_option_value("--stale-days", ...)`, and removing direct argparse `type=int` for stale-days options.
- Updated `tests/test_claude_goal.py::test_invoke_stale_days_rejects_non_integer_before_db_open` to keep non-integer cases separate and added `tests/test_claude_goal.py::test_stale_days_rejects_empty_values_before_db_open` for direct/slash inline-empty and split-empty coverage.
- After-fix QA in `.tmp/claude-goal-t1753-stale-days-empty-value-qa/summary.json` records score `8/8`, decision `adopt_candidate`, and confirms direct plus slash `doctor`/`pause-stale` empty `--stale-days` flows return exit `2`, leave stdout empty, report `goal error: --stale-days requires a value`, avoid argparse `invalid int value`, avoid integer-format errors, avoid DB errors, and print no traceback.
- Verification passed focused stale-days pytest (`6 passed, 129 deselected`), command-cluster pytest (`67 passed, 68 deselected`), full isolated pytest with `PYTHONUTF8=1` (`194 passed`), Ruff check, scoped Ruff format check (`9 files already formatted`), py_compile, `git diff --check` with existing CRLF warnings only, and graph detect risk `0.00`.
- No nested code staging, push, revert, `update_goal`, root product edit, or Hanwoo T-251 retry was performed.

## 2026-06-09 - Codex

- Completed T-1756 as a `claude-goal` quoted invoke objective token-option parse fix in `claude-goal/` on branch `improve/goal-system`, preserving existing nested WIP and the completed T-1755 direct value-option missing-value surface.
- Direct isolated CLI reproduction showed `invoke "objective text" --tokens 10`, `invoke "objective text" --tokens=10`, and quoted-objective invalid/missing token-budget variants failed before set fallback parsing with `goal error: No closing quotation`.
- Confirmed the same quoted objective without options worked, and unquoted word-by-word objective plus token options worked, so the defect was specific to multi-argv shell-quoted objective text followed by token options.
- Root cause: `handle_main_invoke()` round-trips multi-argv input through `shell_command(*args.args)`, which correctly shell-quotes an argv containing spaces, but `_parse_invoke_command()` split that shell-escaped string with plain `.split(maxsplit=1)`, breaking the opening quote before `parse_set_args()` could use `shlex.split()`.
- Fixed `goal/scripts/claude_goal.py` by making `_parse_invoke_command()` parse command boundaries with `shlex.split()` and rebuild `rest` with `shell_command(*parts[1:])`.
- Added `tests/test_claude_goal.py::test_invoke_quoted_objective_preserves_token_options`.
- After-fix QA in `.tmp/claude-goal-t1756-quoted-invoke-token-qa.json` records score `4/4`, decision `adopt_candidate`, and confirms quoted-objective valid split/inline token-budget forms set the intended objective and budget, while invalid/missing values return the specific token-budget usage errors without `No closing quotation` or traceback.
- Verification passed focused regression pytest (`1 passed`), invoke/set cluster pytest (`28 passed, 109 deselected`), full isolated pytest with `PYTHONUTF8=1` (`196 passed`), Ruff check, scoped Ruff format check (`9 files already formatted`), py_compile, `git diff --check` with existing CRLF warnings only, and graph detect risk `0.00`.
- No nested code staging, push, revert, `update_goal`, root product edit, or Hanwoo T-251 retry was performed.

## 2026-06-09 - Codex

- Completed T-1762 as a `claude-goal` set value-option following-option guard fix in `claude-goal/` on branch `improve/goal-system`, preserving existing nested WIP plus the already-recorded T-1761 inline flag-like value-option surface, T-1760 invoke split-form value-option flag-consumption surface, and T-1759 direct boolean explicit-value surface.
- Direct isolated CLI reproduction showed `set objective --token-budget --tokens 10`, slash `invoke objective --token-budget --tokens 10`, `set objective --tokens --budget 10`, slash `invoke objective --tokens --budget 10`, and help-token variants treated the following known option/help token as the budget value and returned `goal error: invalid token budget: '--tokens'`, `--budget`, or `--help`.
- Root cause: `parse_set_args()` only checked for a missing next token; it did not distinguish known set option/help tokens from legitimate budget values before calling `parse_tokens()`.
- Fixed `goal/scripts/claude_goal.py` by adding `SET_VALUE_OPTIONS` / `SET_VALUE_OPTION_BLOCKERS` and rejecting only known set value options plus `-h`/`--help` when they appear in the split value position.
- Added `tests/test_claude_goal.py::test_set_value_options_reject_following_known_options_before_db_open`.
- After-fix QA in `.tmp/claude-goal-t1762-set-option-following-flag-qa.json` records decision `adopt_candidate` and confirms all six direct/slash set following-option probes return exit `2`, leave stdout empty, report `goal error: <option> requires a value`, avoid `invalid token budget`, avoid DB-open masking with `CLAUDE_GOAL_DB` pointing at a directory, and print no traceback.
- Verification passed focused parser pytest (`4 passed, 137 deselected`), manual subprocess probes (`6/6`), full isolated pytest with exported `PYTHONUTF8=1` (`200 passed`), py_compile, Ruff check, scoped Ruff format check (`9 files already formatted`), `git diff --check` with existing CRLF warnings only, and graph detect risk `0.00`.
- One full pytest attempt without exported `PYTHONUTF8` failed only on known Korean Windows path mojibake assertions in child subprocesses; the UTF-8 environment rerun passed.
- No nested code staging, push, revert, `update_goal`, root product edit, or Hanwoo T-251 retry was performed.

## 2026-06-09 - Codex

- Completed T-1765 as a `claude-goal` set inline value-option known-option guard fix in `claude-goal/` on branch `improve/goal-system`, preserving existing nested WIP plus the already-recorded T-1764 direct boolean following-value feedback surface, T-1763 direct split flag-like value-option feedback surface, T-1762 split-form set value-option guard, and T-1761 inline flag-like value-option guard for non-set commands.
- Direct isolated CLI reproduction showed `set objective --token-budget=--tokens`, slash `invoke objective --token-budget=--tokens`, split-argv slash `invoke objective --token-budget=--tokens`, `set objective --tokens=--budget`, slash `invoke objective --tokens=--budget`, and help-token variants returned `goal error: invalid token budget: '--tokens'`, `--budget`, or `--help` instead of the clearer missing-value feedback.
- Official argparse/Click option docs were checked; the chosen policy remains app-level blocking of known option tokens rather than blocking every dash-prefixed value.
- Root cause: T-1762 made split-form `set` budget values check `SET_VALUE_OPTION_BLOCKERS`, but inline `--tokens=...`, `--token-budget=...`, and `--budget=...` paths still called `_validate_set_option_value()` without blocker context before `parse_tokens()`.
- Fixed `goal/scripts/claude_goal.py` by letting `_validate_set_option_value()` pass optional blocked options through to `_validate_option_value()` and applying `SET_VALUE_OPTION_BLOCKERS` to all split and inline set budget value paths.
- Also normalized missing direct main value/boolean option groups to empty sets so the already-recorded T-1764 direct prevalidation path cannot crash on value-only commands.
- Added `tests/test_claude_goal.py::test_set_inline_value_options_reject_known_options_before_db_open`.
- After-fix QA in `.tmp/claude-goal-t1765-set-inline-option-value-qa.json` records decision `adopt_candidate` and confirms all seven direct/slash set inline known-option probes return exit `2`, leave stdout empty, report `goal error: <option> requires a value`, avoid `invalid token budget`, avoid DB-open masking with `CLAUDE_GOAL_DB` pointing at a directory, and print no traceback.
- Verification passed focused parser pytest (`3 passed, 140 deselected`), manual subprocess probes (`7/7`), adjacent repair focused pytest (`4 passed, 140 deselected`), full isolated pytest with exported `PYTHONUTF8=1` (`203 passed`), py_compile, Ruff check, scoped Ruff format check (`9 files already formatted`), `git diff --check` with existing CRLF warnings only, and graph detect risk `0.00`.
- One intermediate full pytest run failed on the adjacent prevalidation TypeError before the repair; the focused repair and full rerun passed.
- No nested code staging, push, revert, `update_goal`, root product edit, or Hanwoo T-251 retry was performed.

## 2026-06-09 - Codex

- Completed T-1766 as a `claude-goal` invoke boolean following-value feedback fix in `claude-goal/` on branch `improve/goal-system`, preserving existing nested WIP plus T-1765 set inline value-option, T-1764 direct boolean following-value, and related parser parity surfaces.
- Direct isolated CLI reproduction showed slash/custom parser boolean options followed by non-option value tokens, including `invoke complete --schema false`, split-argv `invoke complete --schema false`, `invoke contract --markdown false`, `invoke doctor --install false`, `invoke doctor --json false`, `invoke pause-stale --yes false`, and `invoke pause-stale --json false`, returned exit `2` before mutation but reported `goal error: unknown <command> option: false` instead of identifying the boolean option that rejected the value.
- Official argparse/Click option docs were checked; the chosen policy remains app-level validation for exact user feedback.
- Root cause: `_parse_flag_value_command_args()` and `_parse_stale_command_args()` set boolean flags and let the following token fall through to the unknown-option branch; they did not perform the direct-parser-style immediate value check.
- Fixed `goal/scripts/claude_goal.py` by adding `_reject_following_boolean_value()` and applying it to custom slash boolean paths, while preserving valid following option tokens such as `doctor --install --json-output path`.
- Added `tests/test_claude_goal.py::test_invoke_boolean_options_reject_following_values_before_side_effects`.
- After-fix QA in `.tmp/claude-goal-t1766-invoke-boolean-following-value-qa.json` records decision `adopt_candidate` and confirms all seven slash boolean following-value probes return exit `2`, leave stdout empty, report `goal error: <option> does not accept a value`, avoid `unknown ... option`, avoid DB-open masking with `CLAUDE_GOAL_DB` pointing at a directory, and print no traceback.
- Verification passed focused parser pytest after formatting (`3 passed, 142 deselected`), manual subprocess probes (`7/7`), full isolated pytest with exported `PYTHONUTF8=1` (`205 passed`), py_compile, Ruff check, scoped Ruff format check (`9 files already formatted`), `git diff --check` with existing CRLF warnings only, and graph detect risk `0.00`.
- The first format check reported `goal/scripts/claude_goal.py` needed formatting; after `ruff format`, focused and full reruns passed.
- No nested code staging, push, revert, `update_goal`, root product edit, or Hanwoo T-251 retry was performed.
